#############################  MODEL  ###################################

C3F4_CNN(
  (conv1): Sequential(
    (0): Conv2d(103, 380, kernel_size=(7, 7), stride=(1, 1), padding=(3, 3))
    (1): Dropout(p=0.2)
    (2): ReLU(inplace)
  )
  (conv2): Sequential(
    (0): MaxPool2d(kernel_size=2, stride=2, padding=0, dilation=1, ceil_mode=True)
    (1): Conv2d(380, 350, kernel_size=(5, 5), stride=(1, 1), padding=(2, 2))
    (2): Dropout(p=0.2)
    (3): ReLU(inplace)
  )
  (conv3): Sequential(
    (0): MaxPool2d(kernel_size=2, stride=2, padding=0, dilation=1, ceil_mode=True)
    (1): Conv2d(350, 350, kernel_size=(1, 1), stride=(1, 1))
    (2): ReLU(inplace)
  )
  (fc1): Sequential(
    (0): Linear(in_features=22400, out_features=2048, bias=True)
    (1): ReLU(inplace)
  )
  (fc2): Sequential(
    (0): Linear(in_features=2048, out_features=2048, bias=True)
    (1): ReLU(inplace)
  )
  (fc3): Sequential(
    (0): Linear(in_features=2048, out_features=1024, bias=True)
    (1): ReLU(inplace)
  )
  (fc4): Sequential(
    (0): Linear(in_features=1024, out_features=9, bias=True)
  )
  (Softmax): Softmax()
)
